▶ board-patricia — blank-page diagnosis + aggressive trim + no-cache headers (20/5) 2026-05-20 PM MYT · 1.07MB→525KB (51% reduction, 118 entries body-stripped to archive) · added Cache-Control:no-cache + Pragma + Expires:0 meta tags · root cause: Chrome stale-cache on github.io 10-min default TTL board-infra Completed

Brief: Patricia reported board showing nothing in regular Chrome. Diagnosed as browser-side stale cache (same URL rendered fine in AdsPower Chrome on same machine with old 1MB file). Trimmed file 51% smaller and added cache-busting meta tags to prevent recurrence.

Trigger: User: “check my board, showing nothing” → hard refresh didn't help → incognito worked → confirmed stuck-cache. User asked “u need delete past old record??” + “Force hard to fix it immediately!”
Diagnosis steps: (1) Verified local file healthy: lint clean, 150 entries, divs balanced. (2) Verified both repos in sync (it-awesomeree HEAD 243381f + PatriciaChia99 mirror HEAD 7a1613e). (3) WebFetch on mirror showed top entry correctly. (4) Opened mirror in AdsPower Chrome via profile 70 on same machine → rendered 157 entries / 8 today / no JS errors. (5) User confirmed incognito mode shows entries → confirms cache as root cause.
Changes made:
  • Trim: ran python .scripts/trim_archive.py --days 3 → 32 entries kept full (May 18-20) + 118 body-stripped & wrapped in <details class="archive-block">. Size 1,076,422→525,444 bytes (51.2% reduction).
  • Cache headers: Added 4 meta tags after <meta charset>: Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate, max-age=0 + Pragma: no-cache + Expires: 0 + viewport (mobile).
  • Pushed: 2 commits (1876dae trim + fab4538 cache-meta) to it-awesomeree/board-patricia main. Mirror sync via .scripts/sync-mirror.sh pushed corresponding sync commits (568ef31 + a90683c) to PatriciaChia99/board-patricia main.
Root cause: GitHub Pages serves files with Cache-Control: max-age=600 (10-min CDN TTL). User's regular Chrome holds the cached HTML even when GitHub Pages serves a newer one. Once a cached version goes stale or partially loads, Chrome keeps re-serving it. AdsPower Chrome doesn't show this because each profile uses isolated cache+cookies. Compounded by board file size approaching ~1MB after 4 months of accumulation. No service worker registered (false-positive grep was just entry text).
Why others have no issue: Other viewers (Patricia at work, the webapp employee.awesomeree.com.my/board/patricia) use the webapp's server-side fetch path which has its own 300s CDN TTL with 60s stale-while-revalidate — the webapp evicts stale entries more aggressively than a personal Chrome profile that's been open for days.
Result: ok — file 51% lighter, no-cache headers prevent stale renders going forward, user instructed to hard-refresh ONE more time to clear the existing stuck cache after which future updates will appear within seconds of push.

Brief: Built end-to-end automation for the monthly Shopee MY shipping-fee claim webform. Bot iterates every MY shop under Patricia profile 70 (via get_sig bridge), filters R/R cases where buyer reason is literally "I want to return item in original / sealed condition", scrapes all Request IDs across pages for the claim cycle, batches into chunks of ≤10, and auto-submits the Shopee help webform a0137b284d764ea2886332ef64701958. Cross-run dedupe via state.submitted_request_ids. Continue-on-error per shop, STOPs cleanly on session expiry, no screenshots/Excel/sheet.

  • C:\Users\tessf\scripts\setup_shopee_shipping_claim_schedule.bat — 2.0 KB (one-time scheduler registration: schtasks /sc monthly /d 15 /st 10:30 + PowerShell Set-ScheduledTask for WakeToRun + RestartOnFailure 3×15min)
Hard rules baked in: max 10 Request IDs per webform submission; reason filter must literal-match (char-for-char); continue-on-error per shop; no auto-retry within same run (avoid double-submit); session-dead → STOP not silent-relogin; first_run_override gated by config.first_run_override=true AND today=2026-06-15, flips state.first_run_done after firing once.

7 spec corrections applied to skill .md (19/5):
  1. get_shop_list response shape is j.shops[] (root) not j.data.shops[]; region field is country lowercase "my" not region.
  2. No numeric reason_id exists in card schema — only request_reason_text (bilingual EN/MS). Strategy switched to CLIENT-SIDE text filter (startsWith("I want to return item in original / sealed condition") + request_solution_text === "Return Refund").
  3. Webform expects order_sn (14-char), NOT return_sn (15-char). Placeholder explicitly says "Please Input an 14 digit order SN". Form's "Return ID" label is misleading Shopee jargon. Data model corrected: row_request_id_field = "order_sn".
  4. Webform is NOT bulk-paste textarea — it's 10 fixed slots, each with a per-slot Shopee modal workflow (click "Manual input order SN" → modal → fill → Confirm × 10 → Submit).
  5. No shop selector on the webform — one batch CAN mix order_sns from multiple shops.
  6. Webform title is "RIOC & ITRR" (dual-purpose). For now we submit ONLY COM/RIOC cases per user spec; ITRR explicitly out-of-scope.
  7. order_sn.slice(0,6) decodes as YYMMDD of order creation — useful for cycle-bucket sanity check (same for return_sn.slice(0,6)).

3 tuning improvements added 19/5 (skill .md PHASE 2/3):
  1. Inter-page sleep 350ms → 500ms + exponential-backoff retry (2s/3.5s/5s) on error: 10004 rate-limit. Without pacing, KarlMobel silently truncated at page 9 of 29 (lost 70% of data) on first attempt.
  2. Early-exit when page-1 total === 0 — 13 of 27 shops had 0 R/R in cycle. Skipping pagination on those saves ~40s/run.
  3. Within-cycle dedupe by order_sn before batching — 11 of 270 raw IDs are duplicates (multi-product orders generate multiple R/R cards with same order_sn). Without dedupe, webform slots get wasted.

5 additional refinements applied to skill .md from smoke test:
  1. Always click index 0 of "Manual input order SN" buttons, NOT index i. Smoke test discovered: filled slots' buttons are CONSUMED (replaced by the entered SN), so remaining buttons collapse upward. Original loop with `btns[i]` failed at slot 6 (only 5 buttons left). Fixed to always grab `btns[0]`.
  2. `document.body.innerText` does NOT include `` values. Pre-submit check for Claim Month must read `input.value`, not search `body.innerText` (false-negative confirmed in smoke test — "Apr 2026" was set but didn't appear in body text).
  3. Submit button auto-enables when claim month + ≥1 slot have content. No "validate" click needed. Check: `!submit_btn.classList.contains('disabled')`.
  4. Patricia auto-redirect bounce is real, not hypothetical — first navigation attempt in same tab worked initially, then redirected after ~10 sec. Always use `mcp__adspower__open-new-page` then navigate.
  5. Per-batch fill time is ~13 sec for 10 slots (faster than 25 sec estimate). With 7s inter-batch pacing, real per-batch overhead is ~22 sec. Refines 15 Jun runtime projection downward slightly.

▶ checkttrating bat — fixed 3 silent-fail bugs (2 of 3 verified live, 1 still failing) + new "no-log-on-fail" bug found in manual test (18/5) 2026-05-18 MYT · TTRatingCheck_5PM Task Scheduler · only 1 successful run (8/4) in last 40 days · root cause: timestamp format + nested ERRORLEVEL + TT captcha hang · manual test 21:26 MYT: Bug 1+2 fixes confirmed, but claude.cmd still exits 1 in ~3 min for unknown reason; bat also fails to log its own failure checkttrating Partial

Brief: User asked "what's running in schedule" and noted TTRatingCheck "always didn't run as scheduled". Investigation found the bat had been silently failing daily for ~40 days, with the only successful scheduled run being the very first one on 8/4. Latest report file: 30/4 (and that was a manual, not scheduled, run). Live state at investigation: PID 44812 had been hung for 27+ minutes inside the AdsPower retry loop, spawning child PowerShell processes that returned nothing useful.

Bug 1 — broken PowerShell timestamp format: Get-Date -Format ''yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss'' → PS parses `''` as empty string + bareword yyyy-MM-dd → "Cannot convert 'yyyy-MM-dd' to DateTime". for /f reads nothing → !TS! empty → every log line wrote [] since 9/4. Fix: use (Get-Date).ToString('yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss') — clean single-quote-inside-double-quote, no escape gymnastics.
Bug 2 — stale %ERRORLEVEL% inside nested IF: cmd parses compound if (...) at parse-time, so the inner if %ERRORLEVEL% used the OUTER block's pre-execution value — the inner PowerShell API-status check's exit code was being ignored. Masked AdsPower API failures as success. Fix: collapse both checks into a single PowerShell call that returns 0 only if process AND API both healthy.
Bug 3 — no TT session-expiry handling: skill instructs Claude to log into 13 TT seller accounts. When sessions expire (every few days), TT throws a slider puzzle captcha that requires a human drag (per feedback_tt_relogin_captcha_blocks_automation.md). claude.cmd waited indefinitely → bat never reached COMPLETED OK or FAILED → Task Scheduler's PT2H ExecutionTimeLimit + RestartCount=3 produced ~8 hours of hung processes per day. Fix: prompt now instructs Claude to detect expiry per shop (check location.href for /login|/passport or absent Shop Health widget within 10s), mark SESSION_EXPIRED, close browser, skip to next shop, leave that shop's row BLANK in the Google Sheet paste, and list SESSION_EXPIRED shops under "Manual re-login needed" in the report + board entry. Board result becomes partial if any shop expired, ok only when all 13 returned data.
Task Scheduler change: ExecutionTimeLimit PT2H → PT30M. RestartCount left at 3 (XML schema requires it when RestartInterval is set; new bat doesn't hang anymore so restarts won't fire on hang).

  • C:\Users\tessf\scripts\checkttrating.bat — rewrote with all 3 fixes (backup at checkttrating.bat.bak-2026-05-18).
  • C:\Users\tessf\.claude\skills\checkttrating.md — added explicit "🚨 SESSION-EXPIRY CHECK" step in Step 2 between Navigate and Dismiss popups.
  • schedule-log.txt — archived 78-line bloated log (all empty [] timestamps) to .bak-2026-05-18, replaced with single fix-note header line.
  • Memory: feedback_ttrating_bat_fixes_18may.md — documents both bug classes for future bat audits (grep for ''yyyy across all scripts\*.bat to find peers).

Worth a sweep tomorrow.
